<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/html4/strict.dtd">
<html>
	<head>

			<script type="text/javascript">
//global vars (subscriptionorigin,subscriptionid,renew button URL)
var subOrig;
var subId;
var urlrenew = 'http://iws.corel.com/ipmws/redirect/index.jsp?wf=r&pculicenseid=<license>&pcusourceid=<sourceid>&lang=<langcode>&profileid=<profileid>&subscriptionid=<subscriptionid>&serial=<PSN>&<SVRCKS>&x-profileid=<ProfileID>';

function rpt(str) {
	subOrig = extractParam(str, "subscriptionorigin");
	subId = extractParam(str, "subscriptionid");
	//if retail(non-channel) or education, show Redeem Code button
	if (subOrig == '2' && (subId == '2000129' || subId == '2000130' || subId == '2000169' || subId == '2000170')) {
		document.getElementById('redeemacctel').style.display = 'block';
		document.getElementById('purchasecodeast').style.display = 'block';
	}
	else {
		document.getElementById('purchasecodeast').style.display = 'none';
	}
	//if Amazon subscription, hide Progress Bar and apply different Renew link
	if (subId == '2000165' || subId == '2000166' || subId == '2000164' || subId == '2000163') {
		parent.document.getElementById('tdProgress').style.display = 'none';
		urlrenew = 'https://www.amazon.com/yourmembershipsandsubscriptions';
	}
	//if Academic/Education 365 volume subscriptions, hide Renew button
	if (subId == '2000168' || subId == '2000167' || subId == '2000169' || subId == '2000170') {
		document.getElementById('renewacctel').style.display = 'none';
	}
}
function headInit() {
	location = "pcucmd://replacetoken?callback=rpt&string='?subscriptionorigin=<subscriptionorigin>&subscriptionid=<subscriptionid>'";
}
function launchRenewFlow() {
	//if retail(non-channel) subscription add x-updatedsubscriptionid parameter with new value
	if (subOrig == '2' && (subId == '2000129' || subId == '2000130' || subId == '2000169' || subId == '2000170'))
	{
		if (subId == '2000129' || subId == '2000169') {
			urlrenew += '&x-updatedsubscriptionid=900104';
		}
		else if (subId == '2000130' || subId == '2000170') {
			urlrenew += '&x-updatedsubscriptionid=2000124';
		}
	}
	document.location.href = "pcucmd://fullbrowse?URL='" + urlrenew + "'";
	document.getElementById('renewacctel').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('redeemacctel').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('refreshacctel').style.display = 'block';
	document.getElementById('contentbrick').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('purchasecodeast').style.display = 'none';
}
function launchRefreshAcct() {
	location.href = "pcucmd://authenticate?showpsid='true'";
	location.href = "pcucmd://continue";
}
function redeemcode() {
	document.location.href = "pcucmd://fullbrowse?URL='http://iws.corel.com/ipmws/redirect/index.jsp?wf=redeem&pculicenseid=<license>&pcusourceid=<sourceid>&lang=<langcode>&serial=<PSN>&serialtype=<PST>&hfpid=<PCID>&profileid=<profileid>&subscriptionid=<subscriptionid>&<SVRCKS>&x-profileid=<ProfileID>'";
	document.getElementById('renewacctel').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('redeemacctel').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('refreshacctel').style.display = 'block';
	document.getElementById('contentbrick').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('purchasecodeast').style.display = 'none';
}
function closewin() {
	document.location.href = "pcucmd://continue";
}
</script>
		
		<script type="text/javascript" src="../shared/CCC.js"></script>
		<script type="text/javascript">
	
			var itrkid	= 4502;
			var promo	= null;
			var productName = "CorelDRAW Graphics Suite";
			
			function btnHybridRegContinue_OnClick() {
				if (getParamVal("isregistered") == 1) {
					document.location='pcucmd://Continue';
				} else {
					document.location='pcucmd://SetSequence?name=register';
				}
			}
			
			function init() {
				document.location = "pcucmd://ResetCounter";
				document.location.replace('pcucmd://FrameDataLoaded');

				document.location.href = 'pcucmd://AddTrackingData?id=1603733684048&name=workflow&value=trial';
				document.location.href = 'pcucmd://AddTrackingData?id=1603733684048&name=trackingid&value=4502';					
			
		
				if (itrkid != null) {
					document.location.replace('pcucmd://SetCookie?itrkid=' + itrkid);
				}	

				init_trial_page();
			}
		
			function getPCUNVPs(fullList, noAdmin) {
				var nvps = '&licenseid=<license>&sourceid=<sourceid>&lang=es&x-profileid=<ProfileID>&hfpid=<PCID>&NumDays=<NumDays>';

				if (typeof(promo) != "undefined" && promo!=null) {
					document.location = "pcucmd://SetCookie?promo=''";
					
					nvps += "&promo=" + promo;
				}
		
				if (typeof(noAdmin) != "undefined" && !noAdmin) {
					nvps += "&admin=yes";
				}
		
				if (fullList) {
					nvps += "&<SVRCKS>";
				} 

				return nvps;		
			}
			
			function launchStore(noAdmin,fullBrowser,alternativelicenseid) {
				var storeUrl = addGoogleAnalyticsParamsToUrl("http://iws.corel.com/ipmws/redirect/index.jsp?_redirect=pcupurchase" + getPCUNVPs(true, noAdmin));
				if(alternativelicenseid){
					storeUrl += "&alternativelicenseid=" + alternativelicenseid; 
				}
				var url = "pcucmd://browse?URL='" + storeUrl + "'";
				if(arguments.length >= 2 && (fullBrowser == "true" || fullBrowser == true)){
		        		storeUrl += "&fullbrowser=true";
			        	url = "pcucmd://fullbrowse?url='" + storeUrl + "'";
				}
				document.location.href = url;
			}
		
			function launchStoreForTryAndDie(noAdmin,fullBrowser,alternativelicenseid) {
				var storeUrl = addGoogleAnalyticsParamsToUrl("http://iws.corel.com/ipmws/redirect/index.jsp?_redirect=command&buildcode=<SNF>" + getPCUNVPs(true, noAdmin));
				if(alternativelicenseid){
					storeUrl += "&alternativelicenseid=" + alternativelicenseid; 
				}
				var url = "pcucmd://browse?URL='" + storeUrl + "'";
				if(arguments.length >= 2 && (fullBrowser == "true" || fullBrowser == true)){
	        		storeUrl += "&fullbrowser=true";
		        	url = "pcucmd://fullbrowse?url='" + storeUrl + "'";
				}
				document.location.href = url;
			}
			
			function addGoogleAnalyticsParamsToUrl(url){
			   originalUrl = url;
			   try{
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_term","Trial");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_term","Trial");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_medium","IPM");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_medium","IPM");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_source","<license>-<sourceid>");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_source","<license>-<sourceid>");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_campaign","1603733684048");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_campaign","1603733684048");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_content","<PCID>");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_content","<PCID>");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"x-vehicle","Trial");
			   } catch(err) {
			      return originalUrl;
			   }
			   return url;
			}

			function addOrUpdateQStringParam(uri, key, value) {
			  var re = new RegExp("([?&])" + key + "=.*?(&|$)", "i");
			  var separator = uri.indexOf('?') !== -1 ? "&" : "?";
			  if (uri.match(re)) {
			    return uri.replace(re, '$1' + key + "=" + value + '$2');
			  }
			  else {
			    return uri + separator + key + "=" + value;
			  }
			}
		
			function activate() { 
				 location.href = "pcucmd://Activate?admin=yes";
				 location.href = "pcucmd://Next?condition=true";
			}

			function replacePname(){
				if(productName == "null") productName = "Corel";
				content.innerHTML=content.innerHTML.replace("[pname]",productName);
			}

		</script>
	</head>
	<body tabindex="-1" onload="init();replacePname()">
		<div style="text-align:left;">
			<div  id="content">
				
				<div class="workflow_container">
	<h1>Renueve su suscripción.</h1>
	<hr class="tophr">
	<div class="textcol">
		<div id="contentbrick">
		<p>Su suscripción de CorelDRAW está a punto de caducar.</p>
		<p>Renuévela ya para seguir disfrutando de todas las aplicaciones y herramientas más recientes de CorelDRAW Graphics Suite.</p>
		</div>
		<div id="renewacctel">
			<div class="button_container">
				<button class="initiator" accesskey="n" onclick="return launchRenewFlow();" id="idRenew">RE<u>N</u>OVAR AHORA</button>
			</div>
		</div>
		<div id="redeemacctel" style="display: none">
			<div class="button_container">
				<button class="redeemcodebtn" accesskey="d" onclick="return redeemcode();" id="idRedeem">RENOVAR CON CÓ<U>D</U>IGO DE CANJE*</button>
			</div>
		</div>
		<div id="refreshacctel" style="display: none">
			<p>Si has renovado tu suscripción, haz clic en el siguiente vínculo para actualizar el producto con el estado más reciente de Tu cuenta.</p>
			<div class="button_container">
				<button class="initiator" accesskey="e" onclick="launchRefreshAcct()" id="idRefresh">ACTUALIZAR E<U>S</U>TADO</button>
			</div>
		</div>
	</div>
	<div class="imgcol">
		<img src="../shared/images/cdgs2021trialimg2.png" ondragstart="return false;">
	</div>
	<div class="artcreds"><p id="purchasecodeast"><a href="#" onclick="document.location.href='pcucmd://fullbrowse?url=\'https://www.corel.com/partner-locator/\'';">*Adquiere un código de uno de nuestros socios.</a></p></div>
</div>
			</div>

//global vars (subscriptionorigin,subscriptionid,renew button URL)
var subOrig;
var subId;
var urlrenew = 'http://iws.corel.com/ipmws/redirect/index.jsp?wf=r&pculicenseid=<license>&pcusourceid=<sourceid>&lang=<langcode>&profileid=<profileid>&subscriptionid=<subscriptionid>&serial=<PSN>&<SVRCKS>&x-profileid=<ProfileID>';

function rpt(str) {
	subOrig = extractParam(str, "subscriptionorigin");
	subId = extractParam(str, "subscriptionid");
	//if retail(non-channel) or education, show Redeem Code button
	if (subOrig == '2' && (subId == '2000129' || subId == '2000130' || subId == '2000169' || subId == '2000170')) {
		document.getElementById('redeemacctel').style.display = 'block';
		document.getElementById('purchasecodeast').style.display = 'block';
	}
	else {
		document.getElementById('purchasecodeast').style.display = 'none';
	}
	//if Amazon subscription, hide Progress Bar and apply different Renew link
	if (subId == '2000165' || subId == '2000166' || subId == '2000164' || subId == '2000163') {
		parent.document.getElementById('tdProgress').style.display = 'none';
		urlrenew = 'https://www.amazon.com/yourmembershipsandsubscriptions';
	}
	//if Academic/Education 365 volume subscriptions, hide Renew button
	if (subId == '2000168' || subId == '2000167' || subId == '2000169' || subId == '2000170') {
		document.getElementById('renewacctel').style.display = 'none';
	}
}
function headInit() {
	location = "pcucmd://replacetoken?callback=rpt&string='?subscriptionorigin=<subscriptionorigin>&subscriptionid=<subscriptionid>'";
}
function launchRenewFlow() {
	//if retail(non-channel) subscription add x-updatedsubscriptionid parameter with new value
	if (subOrig == '2' && (subId == '2000129' || subId == '2000130' || subId == '2000169' || subId == '2000170'))
	{
		if (subId == '2000129' || subId == '2000169') {
			urlrenew += '&x-updatedsubscriptionid=900104';
		}
		else if (subId == '2000130' || subId == '2000170') {
			urlrenew += '&x-updatedsubscriptionid=2000124';
		}
	}
	document.location.href = "pcucmd://fullbrowse?URL='" + urlrenew + "'";
	document.getElementById('renewacctel').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('redeemacctel').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('refreshacctel').style.display = 'block';
	document.getElementById('contentbrick').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('purchasecodeast').style.display = 'none';
}
function launchRefreshAcct() {
	location.href = "pcucmd://authenticate?showpsid='true'";
	location.href = "pcucmd://continue";
}
function redeemcode() {
	document.location.href = "pcucmd://fullbrowse?URL='http://iws.corel.com/ipmws/redirect/index.jsp?wf=redeem&pculicenseid=<license>&pcusourceid=<sourceid>&lang=<langcode>&serial=<PSN>&serialtype=<PST>&hfpid=<PCID>&profileid=<profileid>&subscriptionid=<subscriptionid>&<SVRCKS>&x-profileid=<ProfileID>'";
	document.getElementById('renewacctel').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('redeemacctel').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('refreshacctel').style.display = 'block';
	document.getElementById('contentbrick').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('purchasecodeast').style.display = 'none';
}
function closewin() {
	document.location.href = "pcucmd://continue";
}

			var itrkid	= 4502;
			var promo	= null;
			var productName = "CorelDRAW Graphics Suite";
			
			function btnHybridRegContinue_OnClick() {
				if (getParamVal("isregistered") == 1) {
					document.location='pcucmd://Continue';
				} else {
					document.location='pcucmd://SetSequence?name=register';
				}
			}
			
			function init() {
				document.location = "pcucmd://ResetCounter";
				document.location.replace('pcucmd://FrameDataLoaded');

				document.location.href = 'pcucmd://AddTrackingData?id=1603733683958&name=workflow&value=trial';
				document.location.href = 'pcucmd://AddTrackingData?id=1603733683958&name=trackingid&value=4502';					
			
		
				if (itrkid != null) {
					document.location.replace('pcucmd://SetCookie?itrkid=' + itrkid);
				}	

				init_trial_page();
			}
		
			function getPCUNVPs(fullList, noAdmin) {
				var nvps = '&licenseid=<license>&sourceid=<sourceid>&lang=es&x-profileid=<ProfileID>&hfpid=<PCID>&NumDays=<NumDays>';

				if (typeof(promo) != "undefined" && promo!=null) {
					document.location = "pcucmd://SetCookie?promo=''";
					
					nvps += "&promo=" + promo;
				}
		
				if (typeof(noAdmin) != "undefined" && !noAdmin) {
					nvps += "&admin=yes";
				}
		
				if (fullList) {
					nvps += "&<SVRCKS>";
				} 

				return nvps;		
			}
			
			function launchStore(noAdmin,fullBrowser,alternativelicenseid) {
				var storeUrl = addGoogleAnalyticsParamsToUrl("http://iws.corel.com/ipmws/redirect/index.jsp?_redirect=pcupurchase" + getPCUNVPs(true, noAdmin));
				if(alternativelicenseid){
					storeUrl += "&alternativelicenseid=" + alternativelicenseid; 
				}
				var url = "pcucmd://browse?URL='" + storeUrl + "'";
				if(arguments.length >= 2 && (fullBrowser == "true" || fullBrowser == true)){
		        		storeUrl += "&fullbrowser=true";
			        	url = "pcucmd://fullbrowse?url='" + storeUrl + "'";
				}
				document.location.href = url;
			}
		
			function launchStoreForTryAndDie(noAdmin,fullBrowser,alternativelicenseid) {
				var storeUrl = addGoogleAnalyticsParamsToUrl("http://iws.corel.com/ipmws/redirect/index.jsp?_redirect=command&buildcode=<SNF>" + getPCUNVPs(true, noAdmin));
				if(alternativelicenseid){
					storeUrl += "&alternativelicenseid=" + alternativelicenseid; 
				}
				var url = "pcucmd://browse?URL='" + storeUrl + "'";
				if(arguments.length >= 2 && (fullBrowser == "true" || fullBrowser == true)){
	        		storeUrl += "&fullbrowser=true";
		        	url = "pcucmd://fullbrowse?url='" + storeUrl + "'";
				}
				document.location.href = url;
			}
			
			function addGoogleAnalyticsParamsToUrl(url){
			   originalUrl = url;
			   try{
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_term","Trial");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_term","Trial");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_medium","IPM");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_medium","IPM");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_source","<license>-<sourceid>");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_source","<license>-<sourceid>");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_campaign","1603733683958");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_campaign","1603733683958");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_content","<PCID>");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_content","<PCID>");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"x-vehicle","Trial");
			   } catch(err) {
			      return originalUrl;
			   }
			   return url;
			}

			function addOrUpdateQStringParam(uri, key, value) {
			  var re = new RegExp("([?&])" + key + "=.*?(&|$)", "i");
			  var separator = uri.indexOf('?') !== -1 ? "&" : "?";
			  if (uri.match(re)) {
			    return uri.replace(re, '$1' + key + "=" + value + '$2');
			  }
			  else {
			    return uri + separator + key + "=" + value;
			  }
			}
		
			function activate() { 
				 location.href = "pcucmd://Activate?admin=yes";
				 location.href = "pcucmd://Next?condition=true";
			}

			function replacePname(){
				if(productName == "null") productName = "Corel";
				content.innerHTML=content.innerHTML.replace("[pname]",productName);
			}

function closewin() {

//base iframe URL
var iframeURL = 'https://ipm.corel.com/products/cdgs/cdgs/nag/retention/cdgssub/sub-rem-to-cdgs2021-and-up-expired/';
function headInit()
{
	//other vars from URL and template
	var langcode = getParamVal("Lang");
	if (langcode == '') {
		langcode = 'en';
	}
	langcode = langcode.toLowerCase();
	var lid = getParamVal("licenseid");
	var sid = getParamVal("SourceID");
	var ndays = getParamVal("NumDays");
	var hfpid = getParamVal("hfpid");
	
	//construct iframe src URL
	iframeURL += langcode + '.html?licenseid=' + lid + '&sourceid=' + sid + '&lang=' + langcode + '&hfpid=' + hfpid + '&daysleft=' + ndays + '&subscriptionid=<subscriptionid>&subscriptionorigin=<subscriptionorigin>&subscriptionseatcount=<subscriptionseatcount>&<SVRCKS>';
	iframeURL = addGoogleAnalyticsParamsToUrl(iframeURL);

	//convert all tokens
	location = "pcucmd://replacetoken?callback='converttokens'&string='" + iframeURL + "'";

	//append the iframe src URL
	document.getElementById('msgiframe').src = iframeURL;
}
function converttokens(str) {
	iframeURL = str;
}
</script>

function closewin() {

//base iframe URL
var iframeURL = 'https://ipm.corel.com/products/cdgs/cdgs/nag/retention/cdgssub/sub-rem-to-cdgs2021-and-up-active/';
function headInit()
{
	//other vars from URL and template
	var langcode = getParamVal("Lang");
	if (langcode == '') {
		langcode = 'en';
	}
	langcode = langcode.toLowerCase();
	var lid = getParamVal("licenseid");
	var sid = getParamVal("SourceID");
	var ndays = getParamVal("NumDays");
	var hfpid = getParamVal("hfpid");
	
	//construct iframe src URL
	iframeURL += langcode + '.html?licenseid=' + lid + '&sourceid=' + sid + '&lang=' + langcode + '&hfpid=' + hfpid + '&daysleft=' + ndays + '&subscriptionid=<subscriptionid>&subscriptionorigin=<subscriptionorigin>&subscriptionseatcount=<subscriptionseatcount>&<SVRCKS>';
	iframeURL = addGoogleAnalyticsParamsToUrl(iframeURL);

	//convert all tokens
	location = "pcucmd://replacetoken?callback='converttokens'&string='" + iframeURL + "'";

	//append the iframe src URL
	document.getElementById('msgiframe').src = iframeURL;
}
function converttokens(str) {
	iframeURL = str;
}

		<script type="text/javascript">
	
			var itrkid	= 4502;
			var promo	= null;
			var productName = "CorelDRAW Graphics Suite";
			
			function btnHybridRegContinue_OnClick() {
				if (getParamVal("isregistered") == 1) {
					document.location='pcucmd://Continue';
				} else {
					document.location='pcucmd://SetSequence?name=register';
				}
			}
			
			function init() {
				document.location = "pcucmd://ResetCounter";
				document.location.replace('pcucmd://FrameDataLoaded');

				document.location.href = 'pcucmd://AddTrackingData?id=1698088455536&name=workflow&value=trial';
				document.location.href = 'pcucmd://AddTrackingData?id=1698088455536&name=trackingid&value=4502';					
			
		
				if (itrkid != null) {
					document.location.replace('pcucmd://SetCookie?itrkid=' + itrkid);
				}	

				init_trial_page();
			}
		
			function getPCUNVPs(fullList, noAdmin) {
				var nvps = '&licenseid=<license>&sourceid=<sourceid>&lang=es&x-profileid=<ProfileID>&hfpid=<PCID>&NumDays=<NumDays>';

				if (typeof(promo) != "undefined" && promo!=null) {
					document.location = "pcucmd://SetCookie?promo=''";
					
					nvps += "&promo=" + promo;
				}
		
				if (typeof(noAdmin) != "undefined" && !noAdmin) {
					nvps += "&admin=yes";
				}
		
				if (fullList) {
					nvps += "&<SVRCKS>";
				} 

				return nvps;		
			}
			
			function launchStore(noAdmin,fullBrowser,alternativelicenseid) {
				var storeUrl = addGoogleAnalyticsParamsToUrl("http://iws.corel.com/ipmws/redirect/index.jsp?_redirect=pcupurchase" + getPCUNVPs(true, noAdmin));
				if(alternativelicenseid){
					storeUrl += "&alternativelicenseid=" + alternativelicenseid; 
				}
				var url = "pcucmd://browse?URL='" + storeUrl + "'";
				if(arguments.length >= 2 && (fullBrowser == "true" || fullBrowser == true)){
		        		storeUrl += "&fullbrowser=true";
			        	url = "pcucmd://fullbrowse?url='" + storeUrl + "'";
				}
				document.location.href = url;
			}
		
			function launchStoreForTryAndDie(noAdmin,fullBrowser,alternativelicenseid) {
				var storeUrl = addGoogleAnalyticsParamsToUrl("http://iws.corel.com/ipmws/redirect/index.jsp?_redirect=command&buildcode=<SNF>" + getPCUNVPs(true, noAdmin));
				if(alternativelicenseid){
					storeUrl += "&alternativelicenseid=" + alternativelicenseid; 
				}
				var url = "pcucmd://browse?URL='" + storeUrl + "'";
				if(arguments.length >= 2 && (fullBrowser == "true" || fullBrowser == true)){
	        		storeUrl += "&fullbrowser=true";
		        	url = "pcucmd://fullbrowse?url='" + storeUrl + "'";
				}
				document.location.href = url;
			}
			
			function addGoogleAnalyticsParamsToUrl(url){
			   originalUrl = url;
			   try{
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_term","Trial");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_term","Trial");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_medium","IPM");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_medium","IPM");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_source","<license>-<sourceid>");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_source","<license>-<sourceid>");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_campaign","1698088455536");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_campaign","1698088455536");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_content","<PCID>");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_content","<PCID>");
			      url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"x-vehicle","Trial");
			   } catch(err) {
			      return originalUrl;
			   }
			   return url;
			}

			function addOrUpdateQStringParam(uri, key, value) {
			  var re = new RegExp("([?&])" + key + "=.*?(&|$)", "i");
			  var separator = uri.indexOf('?') !== -1 ? "&" : "?";
			  if (uri.match(re)) {
			    return uri.replace(re, '$1' + key + "=" + value + '$2');
			  }
			  else {
			    return uri + separator + key + "=" + value;
			  }
			}
		
			function activate() { 
				 location.href = "pcucmd://Activate?admin=yes";
				 location.href = "pcucmd://Next?condition=true";
			}

			function replacePname(){
				if(productName == "null") productName = "Corel";
				content.innerHTML=content.innerHTML.replace("[pname]",productName);
			}

			<script type="text/javascript">
//global vars (subscriptionorigin,subscriptionid,renew button URL)
var subOrig;
var subId;
var urlrenew = 'http://iws.corel.com/ipmws/redirect/index.jsp?wf=r&pculicenseid=<license>&pcusourceid=<sourceid>&lang=<langcode>&profileid=<profileid>&subscriptionid=<subscriptionid>&serial=<PSN>&<SVRCKS>&x-profileid=<ProfileID>';

function rpt(str) {
	subOrig = extractParam(str, "subscriptionorigin");
	subId = extractParam(str, "subscriptionid");
	//if retail(non-channel) or education, show Redeem Code button
	if (subOrig == '2' && (subId == '2000129' || subId == '2000130' || subId == '2000169' || subId == '2000170')) {
		document.getElementById('redeemacctel').style.display = 'block';
		document.getElementById('purchasecodeast').style.display = 'block';
	}
	else {
		document.getElementById('purchasecodeast').style.display = 'none';
	}
	//if Amazon subscription, hide Progress Bar and apply different Renew link
	if (subId == '2000165' || subId == '2000166' || subId == '2000164' || subId == '2000163') {
		parent.document.getElementById('tdProgress').style.display = 'none';
		urlrenew = 'https://www.amazon.com/yourmembershipsandsubscriptions';
	}
	//if Academic/Education 365 volume subscriptions, hide Renew button
	if (subId == '2000168' || subId == '2000167' || subId == '2000169' || subId == '2000170') {
		document.getElementById('renewacctel').style.display = 'none';
	}
}
function headInit() {
	location = "pcucmd://replacetoken?callback=rpt&string='?subscriptionorigin=<subscriptionorigin>&subscriptionid=<subscriptionid>'";
}
function launchRenewFlow() {
	//if retail(non-channel) subscription add x-updatedsubscriptionid parameter with new value
	if (subOrig == '2' && (subId == '2000129' || subId == '2000130' || subId == '2000169' || subId == '2000170'))
	{
		if (subId == '2000129' || subId == '2000169') {
			urlrenew += '&x-updatedsubscriptionid=900104';
		}
		else if (subId == '2000130' || subId == '2000170') {
			urlrenew += '&x-updatedsubscriptionid=2000124';
		}
	}
	document.location.href = "pcucmd://fullbrowse?URL='" + urlrenew + "'";
	document.getElementById('renewacctel').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('redeemacctel').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('refreshacctel').style.display = 'block';
	document.getElementById('contentbrick').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('purchasecodeast').style.display = 'none';
}
function launchRefreshAcct() {
	location.href = "pcucmd://authenticate?showpsid='true'";
	location.href = "pcucmd://continue";
}
function redeemcode() {
	document.location.href = "pcucmd://fullbrowse?URL='http://iws.corel.com/ipmws/redirect/index.jsp?wf=redeem&pculicenseid=<license>&pcusourceid=<sourceid>&lang=<langcode>&serial=<PSN>&serialtype=<PST>&hfpid=<PCID>&profileid=<profileid>&subscriptionid=<subscriptionid>&<SVRCKS>&x-profileid=<ProfileID>'";
	document.getElementById('renewacctel').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('redeemacctel').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('refreshacctel').style.display = 'block';
	document.getElementById('contentbrick').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('purchasecodeast').style.display = 'none';
}
function closewin() {
	document.location.href = "pcucmd://continue";
}
</script>

function onPageContinue()
{
  location='pcucmd://SetRegConfirmationCode?offline=true';
  location='pcucmd://Next?condition=yes';
}

function OnTxtFieldChanging()
{
		var oKey = document.getElementById("txtCode");
		var sResult = "false";

		if (oKey != null)
		{
			if (ValidateSerial(oKey.value))
			{
				sResult = "true";
			}

			location = "pcucmd://StoreParam?code=" + oKey.value;
		}

		location="pcucmd://CanContinue?enable=" + sResult;

}

<script language="javascript">
	<!--

	function onpageload()

	function showhide(el)

	function OnBack()
	{
		var strSerial = getCookie("serial");
		if ((strSerial != null) && (strSerial != ""))
		{
			location="pcucmd://SetKey?admin=yes&key="+strSerial;
			deleteCookie("serial");
		}
		location="pcucmd://previous";
	}

	function callCancel() {
		var strSerial = getCookie("serial");
		if ((strSerial != null) && (strSerial != "")) {
			location = "pcucmd://SetKey?admin=yes&key=" + strSerial;
			deleteCookie("serial");
		}
		location = "pcucmd://cancel?confirm=no";
	}

	//clear error message field
	function clearErrorMsg() {
		error_msg.style.display = "none";
	}

	function preValidate() {
		//make sure username or password are not empty
		if (username.value == "" || password.value == "") {
			var errorstr_empty = document.getElementById('errorstr_empty').innerText;
			processerror(errorstr_empty);
		}
		//make sure username is a string and lower-case
		else {
			username.value = username.value.toString().toLowerCase();
		}
	}

	//error handling
	function processerror(strError) {
		g_bError = true;
		var nIndex = strError.indexOf("|");
		var strErrorDesc = strError;
		var strErrorcode;
		if (nIndex >= 0) {
			strErrorDesc = strErrorDesc.substr(nIndex + 1);
			strErrorCode = strError.substr(0, nIndex);
		}
		error_msg.style.display = "block";
		error_msg.innerHTML = strErrorDesc;
	}

	//new error handling for pcucmd SetKey (July2021)
	function processnewsnerror() {
		g_bError = true;
		var errstr = document.getElementById('errorstr_setkeyerr').innerHTML;
		error_msg.style.display = "block";
		error_msg.innerHTML = errstr;
	}

	//serial number validation every time a key is pressed inside the serial number input field
	function OnSerialChanging()
	{
		var pKey = document.getElementById("txtKey");
		if (null == pKey) {
			return;
		}
		var strKey = removeAllSpaces(pKey.value);
		var bSerial = ValidateSerial(strKey);
		//enable auth button
		document.getElementById('btnActivateOnline').disabled = !bSerial;
		return;
	}

	//submitting SN
	function OnAuthenticateSN()
	{
		g_bError = false;
		location = "pcucmd://SetKey?admin=yes&key=" + removeAllSpaces(txtKey.value) + "&showerror='no'&onerror='processnewsnerror'";
		if (g_bError == false)
		{
			//also validate credentials
			if (username.disabled == false && password.disabled == false)
			{
				//creating acct
				if (haveacct.checked == false) {
					location.href = "pcucmd://CallScriptFunc?funcname=validate";
				}
				else {
					location.href = "pcucmd://CallScriptFunc?funcname=logon";
				}
			}
			//just sn
			else {
				location.href = "pcucmd://CallScriptFunc?funcname=snsuccess";
			}
		}
	}
	
	function CheckCred(type,input) {
		var str;
		//email
		if (type == 'e') {
			str = /\S+@\S+\.\S+/;
		}
		//password
		else if (type == 'p') {
			str = /^[A-Za-z0-9=\+\._,<>-`\*\^"!\?@&\$%#~\|';:{}\(\)\[\]\/\\]{6,32}$/;
		}
		if (str != undefined)
		{
			if(str.test(input)) {
				return true;
			}
			else {
				return false;
			}
		}
	}

	function validate()
	{
		clearErrorMsg();
		//assume good
		g_bError = false;
		preValidate();
		var success = true;
		var errors = "";
		if (g_bError == false)
		{
			if( !CheckCred('e',username.value)) {
				success = false;
				errors += document.getElementById('errorstr_bademail').innerText + "\n";
			}
			if( !CheckCred('p',password.value)) {
				success = false;
				errors += document.getElementById('errorstr_badpass').innerText + "\n";
			}
			if( !CheckCred('p',confirmpassword.value)) {
				success = false;
				errors += document.getElementById('errorstr_badpassconf').innerText + "\n";
			}
			if(password.value != confirmpassword.value) {					
				success = false;
				errors += document.getElementById('errorstr_passmismatch').innerText + "\n";
			}
			if(success == true) {
				CreateAccount();
			}
			else {
				processerror(errors);
			}
		}
	}

	function CreateAccount()
	{
		var SubscriptionID = getCookie("SubscriptionID");
		var crit = document.getElementById("CritSWUpdateCheckbox");
		var custR = document.getElementById("CorelResearchCheckbox");
		var vFlag = 0;
		
		if(crit.checked) {
			vFlag = vFlag | 3;
		}
		if(custR.checked) {
			vFlag = vFlag | 16;
		}

		var Nickname = "";
		var Language = getParamVal("language");

		g_bError = false;		
		location = "pcucmd://createAccount?username='" + username.value + "'&password='" + password.value + "'&nickname='" + Nickname + "'&langcode='" + Language +  "'&countrycode='" + document.getElementById("countrySelector").value + "'&flags='" + vFlag + "'&onerror=processerror";

		if (!g_bError) {	
			sendEmailValidation();
			logon();
		}
	}
	
	function OnPrivacy() {
		location = "pcucmd://fullbrowse?url='<CorelComServer>/privacy'";
	}

	//logging in
	function logon() {
		clearErrorMsg();
		//assume good
		g_bError = false;
		preValidate();
		if (g_bError == false)
		{
			location.href = "pcucmd://authenticate?username='" + username.value + "'&password='" + password.value + "'&showpsid='true'&onerror='processerror'";
			if (g_bError == false) {
				loginsuccess();
			}
		}
	}

	//submitting sn
	function snsuccess() {
		//assume good
		g_bError = false;
		location.href = "pcucmd://authenticate?showpsid='true'&onerror='processerror'";
		if (g_bError == false) {
			location = "pcucmd://Next";
		}
	}
	
	//successfully logged in
	function loginsuccess() {
		location.href = "pcucmd://SetCookie?lusr=''";
		setCookie("lusr","");
		location = "pcucmd://Next";
	}
	-->
</script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
var email = '';
var langcode = 'en';
var wfquery = '';
var hashedemail = '';
function rpt(str) {
	email = str;
}
function onpageload()
{
	location = 'pcucmd://FrameDataLoaded';
	var classification = getParamVal("classification");
	var subscriptionid = getParamVal("subscriptionid");
	var alreadyexist = getParamVal("alreadyexist");
	
	//fill in user email and SN
	location = "pcucmd://replacetoken?callback='rpt'&string='<UserID>'";
	if (!email) {
		location.href = "pcucmd://Continue";
	}
	//if email is available,encrypt it and do some GA pinging
	else
	{
		email = email.toLowerCase();
		if (typeof(sha256Generator) !== 'undefined') {
			hashedemail = sha256Generator.hash(email);
		}

		//get the language from path (EN default)
		var path = window.location.href;
		var langpos = path.indexOf("/MessageCache");
		if (langpos != -1) {
			langpos = langpos-2;
			langcode = path.substring(langpos,langpos+2);
			langcode = langcode.toLowerCase();
			
			//get path from /Messages onwards (encoded)
			var wfpos = path.indexOf("/Messages");
			wfquery = encodeURIComponent(path.substring(wfpos));
		}
		if (langcode == 'es') {
			langcode = 'la';
		}
		else if (langcode == 'cs') {
			langcode = 'cn';
		}
		else if (langcode == 'ct') {
			langcode = 'tw';
		}
		else if (langcode == 'tr' || langcode == 'sv') {
			langcode = 'en';
		}
	}

	//populate dynamic content elements
	var sn = getParamVal("serial");
	sn = sn.toUpperCase();
	document.getElementById('user_email').innerHTML = email;
	document.getElementById('user_sn').innerHTML = sn;
	document.getElementById('user_email1').innerHTML = email;

	//if previously signed in with single SN
	if (alreadyexist == 'true') {
		//proper heading
		document.getElementById('hd3').style.display = 'block';

		//hide or show content
		document.getElementById('freeupgrade').style.display = 'block';
	}
	else if (classification == '2' || alreadyexist == 'multi') {
		location.href = "pcucmd://Continue";
	}
	//unverified or pirate
	else if (classification == '1') {
		//proper heading
		document.getElementById('hd2').style.display = 'block';
		
		//hide or show content
		document.getElementById('unverified').style.display = 'block';
	}
	//trial
	else if (classification == '0') {
		//proper heading
		document.getElementById('hd1').style.display = 'block';

		//hide or show content
		document.getElementById('signedin_trial').style.display = 'block';
		document.getElementById('user_email').style.display = 'block';
	}
	//standard
	else {
		document.getElementById('hd1').style.display = 'block';

		//hide or show content
		document.getElementById('user_email').style.display = 'block';
		document.getElementById('signedin').style.display = 'block';
		document.getElementById('signedin_prod').style.display = 'block';
	}

	//run visibility on main license to see if we are showing S1/biztrial elements (NOT legacy Perp trial sourceids)
	location.href = "pcucmd://validate?param=/productmanifest/licenseinfolist/licenseinfo[((@licenseid='540111147' and @sourceid!='910035') or (@licenseid='540111148' and @sourceid!='810034')) and (@serialtype='3' or @serialtype='15' or (@serialtype='0' and string-length(@serialnum)>'28'))]";
	location.href = "pcucmd://CallScriptFunc?condition=true&funcname=showelements&param=s1biz";

	//run visibility on main license to see if we are showing biztrial elements (biz sourceids)
	location.href = "pcucmd://validate?param=/productmanifest/licenseinfolist/licenseinfo[(@licenseid='540111147' and @sourceid='110037') or (@licenseid='540111148' and @sourceid='010036') and @classification!='0']";
	location.href = "pcucmd://CallScriptFunc?condition=true&funcname=showelements&param=biz";
}

function showelements(eltype)
{
	//make sure element is there (new S1 bullet point)
	if (!document.getElementById('s1bullet')) {
		return false;
	}
	document.getElementById('s1bullet').style.display = '';
	if (eltype == 'biz')
	{
		//make sure element is there (new business trial icon section)
		if (!document.getElementById('bizsection')) {
			return false;
		}
		document.getElementById('bizsection').style.display = 'block';
		document.getElementById('hd1').style.display = 'none';
		document.getElementById('hd2').style.display = 'none';
		document.getElementById('hd3').style.display = 'none';
		document.getElementById('hd4').style.display = 'block';
	}
}

function nextstep () {
	//ping GA for view tracking
	document.getElementById('omnit').src = addGoogleAnalyticsParamsToUrl('https://ipm.corel.com/products/tracking/index.html?page_path=' + wfquery + '&site_key=coreldraw.com&ga-user-id=' + hashedemail,'signin_confirmation','1603733684135');
	//go to fullbrowser reg thank you page and continue launching app
	location.href = "pcucmd://fullbrowse?url='https://www.coreldraw.com/" + langcode + "/product/coreldraw/registration-thank-you.html?ga-user-id=" + hashedemail + "&hwid=<hwid>'&showatfront='false'";
	location = 'pcucmd://continue';
}

function subsupportlink() {
	location.href = "pcucmd://fullbrowse?url='https://www.coreldraw.com/authenticationsupport'";
	return false;
}
</script>

			<script language="javascript">
				var css_lang = "ES";
				var productName = "CorelDRAW Graphics Suite";
				function changeSchedule(newInterval) {
					document.location.href="pcucmd://SetSchedule?NumDays=" + newInterval;
				}

				function optionalReg_Onload() {
					if (getParamVal('regsuppressoffline') == 'true') {
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://FrameDataLoaded';
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://Continue';
					} else {
						var newLaunchCount=parseInt(getParamVal("offerLoadCount"));
						if (isNaN(newLaunchCount)) {
							newLaunchCount=0;
						}

						newLaunchCount=newLaunchCount+1;
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://AddTrackingData?id=1241638404862&name=workflow&value=registration';
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://AddTrackingData?id=1241638404862&name=actionid&value=123';
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://AddTrackingData?id=1241638404862&name=trackingid&value=4501';					
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://AddTrackingData?id=1241638404862&name=invokedfrom&value=' + getParamVal("invokedfrom");
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://AddTrackingData?id=1241638404862&name=regtype&value=' + getParamVal("regtype");
						
						document.location.href="pcucmd://FrameDataLoaded";
						document.location.href="pcucmd://SetCookie?offerloadcount="+newLaunchCount;
						
					}
				}

				function replacePname(){
					if(productName == "null") productName = "Corel";
					content.innerHTML=content.innerHTML.replace("[pname]",productName);
				}

				function processMenu(optionValue){
					
					if ( (null == optionValue) || (undefined == optionValue) ){
						optionValue = "register";
					}
					if (optionValue == "register"){
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://SetSequence?name=register';
						return;
					}
					
					if (optionValue == "doNotRemind"){
						changeSchedule(-1);
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://Cancel?confirm=no'
						return;
					}
					
					if (!isNaN(optionValue)){
						changeSchedule(optionValue);
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://Cancel?confirm=no';
						return;
					}
					
					document.location.href = 'pcucmd://SetSequence?name=register';
				}
				
				function OnRegisterToday() {
					document.location.href='pcucmd://Connect';
					document.location.href='pcucmd://SetSequence?name=register_welcome&condition=true';
					return false;
				}
			</script>
		</head>

			<script language="javascript">
				var css_lang = "ES";
				var productName = "CorelDRAW Graphics Suite";
				function changeSchedule(newInterval) {
					document.location.href="pcucmd://SetSchedule?NumDays=" + newInterval;
				}

				function optionalReg_Onload() {
					if (getParamVal('regsuppressoffline') == 'true') {
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://FrameDataLoaded';
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://Continue';
					} else {
						var newLaunchCount=parseInt(getParamVal("offerLoadCount"));
						if (isNaN(newLaunchCount)) {
							newLaunchCount=0;
						}

						newLaunchCount=newLaunchCount+1;
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://AddTrackingData?id=1241638404845&name=workflow&value=registration';
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://AddTrackingData?id=1241638404845&name=actionid&value=123';
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://AddTrackingData?id=1241638404845&name=trackingid&value=4501';					
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://AddTrackingData?id=1241638404845&name=invokedfrom&value=' + getParamVal("invokedfrom");
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://AddTrackingData?id=1241638404845&name=regtype&value=' + getParamVal("regtype");
						
						document.location.href="pcucmd://FrameDataLoaded";
						document.location.href="pcucmd://SetCookie?offerloadcount="+newLaunchCount;
						
					}
				}

				function replacePname(){
					if(productName == "null") productName = "Corel";
					content.innerHTML=content.innerHTML.replace("[pname]",productName);
				}

				function processMenu(optionValue){
					
					if ( (null == optionValue) || (undefined == optionValue) ){
						optionValue = "register";
					}
					if (optionValue == "register"){
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://SetSequence?name=register';
						return;
					}
					
					if (optionValue == "doNotRemind"){
						changeSchedule(-1);
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://Cancel?confirm=no'
						return;
					}
					
					if (!isNaN(optionValue)){
						changeSchedule(optionValue);
						document.location.href = 'pcucmd://Cancel?confirm=no';
						return;
					}
					
					document.location.href = 'pcucmd://SetSequence?name=register';
				}
				
				function OnRegisterToday() {
					document.location.href='pcucmd://Connect';
					document.location.href='pcucmd://SetSequence?name=register_welcome&condition=true';
					return false;
				}
			</script>
		</head>

function onpageload()
{
	document.location.replace('pcucmd://FrameDataLoaded');
	var newURL = 'pcucmd://fullbrowse?URL="http://iws.corel.com/ipmws/redirect/index.jsp' + getParamString();
	var triggerval = getParamVal("trigger");
	if (triggerval > 0){
		newURL += '&utm_term=Trial&utm_medium=IPM&utm_source=<license>-<sourceid>&utm_content=Headernavbuynow';
	}
	var fullbrowser = getParamVal("fullbrowser");
	if (fullbrowser == '') {
		newURL += '&fullbrowser=true';
	}
	document.location.replace(newURL);
	if (triggerval  == -1) {
		location='pcucmd://setlastsequence';
	}
	else {
		location='pcucmd://cancel?confirm=no';
	}
	document.location.replace('pcucmd://FrameDataLoaded');
}

				for (i = 0; i < 5; i++)
				{
					var oField = document.getElementById("txtInstCode" + (i + 1));
					if (oField != null)
						oField.value = ss[i].toUpperCase();
				}
			}
		}
		sCode = getParamVal("serial");
		if ((sCode != null) && (sCode.length > 0))
		{
			var oKey = document.getElementById("txtKey");
			if (null != oKey)
			{
				oKey.readOnly = true;
				oKey.value = sCode.toUpperCase();
				oKey.style.background = '#fcfcfc';
			}
		}
		sCode = getParamVal("SourceID");
		var sNumDays = getParamVal("NumDays");
		if (sCode != null)
		{
			var oField = document.getElementById("txtID");
			if (oField != null)
			{
				if (sNumDays != null)
					sCode = sCode + " " + sNumDays;

				oField.value = sCode;
			}
		}
	}

	function OnTxtFieldChanging()
	{
		var oAct = document.getElementById("txtActivationCode");

		var strAct = "";

		if (oAct != null)
		{
			strAct = removeAllSpaces(oAct.value);
			location = "pcucmd://StoreParam?activationcode=" + strAct;
		}

		if (ValidateActCode(strAct))
		{
			location="pcucmd://CanContinue?enable=true";
		}
		else
		{
			location="pcucmd://CanContinue?enable=false";
		}
	}
	
	function OnBack()
	{
		var strSerial = getCookie("serial");
		if ((strSerial != null) && (strSerial != ""))
		{
			location="pcucmd://SetKey?admin=yes&key="+strSerial;
			deleteCookie("serial");
		}
		location="pcucmd://previous";
	}
	function callCancel() {
	    var strSerial = getCookie("serial");
	    if ((strSerial != null) && (strSerial != "")) {
	        location = "pcucmd://SetKey?admin=yes&key=" + strSerial;
	        deleteCookie("serial");
	    }
	    location = "pcucmd://cancel?confirm=no";
	}

	<wm:workflowmessage
	    wm:name="enter_sn_enter_credentials_page"
	    id='1625473630325'
	    
	    
	    modified-timestamp='1631197033000'
	    >
		<contents>
			<content type="" localpath="1625473630325\body.htm">
			    <![CDATA[
				<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.01 Transitional//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/html4/strict.dtd">		    
				<html>
					<head>
						<meta http-equiv="MSThemeCompatible" content="yes">
						<meta HTTP-EQUIV="Content-Type" CONTENT="text/html; charset=UTF-8">
						
								<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" href='..\genericSkin\1248383926732,16.txt.css'/>
								
						
							
							<script src="../shared/ccc.js"></script>
<script language="javascript">
	//global vars
	var txtKey,username,password,selsn,selsignin,error_msg,pcubtncontinue;
	var g_bError = false;
	var g_tokens;
	function rpt(tokens) {
		g_tokens = tokens;
	}

	function onpageload()
	{
		txtKey = document.getElementById('txtKey');
		username = document.getElementById("username");
		password = document.getElementById("password");
		selsn = document.getElementById("selsn");
		selsignin = document.getElementById("selsignin");
		error_msg = document.getElementById('error_msg');
		pcubtncontinue = parent.document.getElementById('pcubtncontinue');

		//if returning user
		/*var lastUser = getParamVal("lusr");
		if ("" != lastUser) {
			username.style.background = 'white';
			username.value = lastUser;
		}*/
		location="pcucmd://CanContinue?enable=false";
		location = 'pcucmd://FrameDataLoaded';
	}

	//is user logging in or submitting SN
	function nextstep() {
		//submitting SN
		if (selsn.checked == true) {
			OnAuthenticateSN();
		}
		//logging in
		else if (selsignin.checked == true) {
			logon();
		}
	}

	//serial number checkbox action
	function enablesn(el) {
		//sn checkbox was checked
		if (el.checked == true) {
			txtKey.disabled = false;
		}
		//sn checkbox was unchecked
		else {
			txtKey.disabled = true;
			//if both were unchecked, disable continue btn
			if (document.getElementById('selsignin').checked == false) {
				pcubtncontinue.disabled = true;
			}
			else {
				pcubtncontinue.disabled = false;
			}
		}
	}

	//signin checkbox action
	function enablesi(el) {
		//sign-in checkbox was checked
		if (el.checked == true) {		
			username.disabled = false;
			password.disabled = false;
			//if sn checkbox is unchecked
			if (document.getElementById('selsn').checked == false) {
				pcubtncontinue.disabled = false;
			}
		}
		//sign-in checkbox was unchecked
		else {
			username.disabled = true;
			password.disabled = true;
			//if both were unchecked, disable continue btn
			if (document.getElementById('selsn').checked == false) {
				pcubtncontinue.disabled = true;
			}
		}	
	}
	
	//clear error message field
	function clearErrorMsg() {
		error_msg.style.display = "none";
	}

	function preValidate() {
		//make sure username or password are not empty
		if (username.value == "" || password.value == "") {
			var errorstr_empty = document.getElementById('errorstr_empty').innerText;
			processerror(errorstr_empty);
		}
		//make sure username is a string and lower-case
		else {
			username.value = username.value.toString().toLowerCase();
		}
	}

	//error handling
	function processerror(strError) {
		g_bError = true;
		var nIndex = strError.indexOf("|");
		var strErrorDesc = strError;
		var strErrorcode;
		if (nIndex >= 0) {
			strErrorDesc = strErrorDesc.substr(nIndex + 1);
			strErrorCode = strError.substr(0, nIndex);
		}
		error_msg.style.display = "block";
		error_msg.innerHTML = strErrorDesc;
	}

	//new error handling for pcucmd SetKey (July2021)
	function processnewsnerror() {
		g_bError = true;
		var errstr = document.getElementById('errorstr_setkeyerr').innerHTML;
		error_msg.style.display = "block";
		error_msg.innerHTML = errstr;
	}

	//serial number validation every time a key is pressed inside the serial number input field
	function OnSerialChanging()
	{
		var pKey = document.getElementById("txtKey");
		if (null == pKey) {
			return;
		}
		var strKey = removeAllSpaces(pKey.value);
		var bSerial = ValidateSerial(strKey);
		//enable continue button
		pcubtncontinue.disabled = !bSerial;
		return;
	}

	//submitting SN
	function OnAuthenticateSN()
	{
		g_bError = false;
		location = "pcucmd://SetKey?admin=yes&key=" + removeAllSpaces(txtKey.value) + "&showerror='no'&onerror='processnewsnerror'";
		if (g_bError == false)
		{
			//also validate credentials scenario
			if (username.disabled == false && password.disabled == false) {
				location.href = "pcucmd://CallScriptFunc?funcname=logon&condition=true";
			}
			//just sn
			else {
				location.href = "pcucmd://CallScriptFunc?funcname=snsuccess&condition=true";
			}
		}
	}

	//logging in
	function logon() {
		clearErrorMsg();
		//assume good
		g_bError = false;
		preValidate();
		if (g_bError == false)
		{
			location.href = "pcucmd://authenticate?username='" + username.value + "'&password='" + password.value + "'&showpsid='true'&onerror='processerror'";
			if (g_bError == false) {
				loginsuccess();
			}
		}
	}

	//submitting sn
	function snsuccess() {
		//assume good
		g_bError = false;
		location.href = "pcucmd://authenticate?showpsid='true'&onerror='processerror'";
		if (g_bError == false) {
			location = "pcucmd://Next";
		}
	}
	
	//successfully logged in
	function loginsuccess() {
		location.href = "pcucmd://SetCookie?lusr=''";
		setCookie("lusr","");
		location = "pcucmd://Next";
	}
</script>

<td><button style='overflow:visible;width:100%' class='buttonBar' type='submit' accessKey='o' id='pcubtncontinue' name='pcubtncontinue'  onclick="document.location='pcucmd://CallScriptFunc?funcname=nextstep'">C<u>o</u>ntinuar</button></td>

							<div class="workflow_container">
	<h1>Edición de tus credenciales</h1>
	<hr>
	<p>Si necesitas modificar las credenciales del producto, indica aquí la nueva información. Al cambiar estas opciones avanzadas de configuración, podría verse afectado el rendimiento de la aplicación.</p>
	<table class="selsntable" cellpadding="3" cellspacing="3" border="0">
		<tr>
			<td><input id="selsn" type="checkbox" onclick="enablesn(this);" checked/></td>
			<td><label for="selsn">Recientemente combiné dos números de serie de producto o actualicé un número de serie y deseo usar ese número de serie para este producto.</label>
		</tr>
	</table>
	<div>
		<label for="txtKey" class="inputlabel">Número de <U>s</U>erie</label>

//send to mini or full browser
function sendbrowser(type,url) {
	if (type == 'mini') {
		document.location.href = 'pcucmd://browse?url=\'' + url + '\'&width=1000&height=800';
	}
	else {
		document.location.href = 'pcucmd://fullbrowse?url=\'' + url + '\'';
	}
}
function onpageload() {
	location = 'pcucmd://FrameDataLoaded';
}
function addOrUpdateQStringParam(uri, key, value) {
  var re = new RegExp("([?&])" + key + "=.*?(&|$)", "i");
  var separator = uri.indexOf('?') !== -1 ? "&" : "?";
  if (uri.match(re)) {
    return uri.replace(re, '$1' + key + "=" + value + '$2');
  }
  else {
    return uri + separator + key + "=" + value;
  }
}
function addGoogleAnalyticsParamsToUrl(url)
{
	originalUrl = url;
	try{
		url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_term","piracyretail");
		url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_term","piracyretail");
		url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_medium","IPM");
		url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_medium","IPM");
		url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_source","<License>-<SourceID>");
		url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_source","<License>-<SourceID>");
		url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_campaign","1599453161264");
		url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_campaign","1599453161264");
		url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"utm_content","<PCID>");
		url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"ctm_content","<PCID>");
		url = addOrUpdateQStringParam(url,"x-vehicle","piracyretail");
		var lidsid = window.location.pathname;
		var lidsidpos = lidsid.indexOf("/Corel/Messages/");
		if (lidsidpos != -1) {
			lidsidpos = lidsidpos + 16;
			lidsid = lidsid.substring(lidsidpos, lidsidpos + 16);
			url = url.replace(/<License>-<SourceID>/gi, lidsid);
		}
	}
	catch(err) {
		return originalUrl;
		var lidsid = window.location.pathname;
		var lidsidpos = lidsid.indexOf("/Corel/Messages/");
		if (lidsidpos != -1) {
			lidsidpos = lidsidpos + 16;
			lidsid = lidsid.substring(lidsidpos, lidsidpos + 16);
			url = url.replace(/<License>-<SourceID>/gi, lidsid);
		}
	}
	return url;
}

	<wm:workflowmessage

<script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
	//global vars
	var username,password,confirmpassword,haveacct,error_msg;
	var g_bError = false;
	var g_tokens;
	function rpt(tokens) {
		g_tokens = tokens;
	}

	function onpageload()
	{
		username = document.getElementById("username");
		password = document.getElementById("password");
		confirmpassword = document.getElementById('passwordConf')
		haveacct = document.getElementById('haveacct');
		error_msg = document.getElementById('error_msg');
		
		//privacy checkboxes must be unchecked if marked in registry
		location.href = "pcucmd://validate?param=/registry/regkey[@name='hkcu/software/corel/pcu']/regval[@name='privacydefault'][@value='1']";
		location.href = "pcucmd://CallScriptFunc?condition=true&funcname=privcheckboxes";
		
		var serialtype = getParamVal("serialtype");
		var heading = 'hd1';
		//if subscription user
		if (serialtype == '15')
		{
			heading = 'hd2';
			showhide('subsc');
		}
		//non-subscription user
		else
		{
			var prodver = parseInt(getParamVal("productversion"));
			if (isNaN(prodver) == true) {
				prodver = '23.0';
			}
			else {
				prodver = prodver.toFixed(1);
			}
			//default is Graphics Suite
			var prodregpath = 'coreldraw/' + prodver + '/ipm_cdgs';

			var licid = getParamVal("pculicenseid");
			//2021 Essentials
			if (licid == '540111152' || licid == '540111146') {
				prodregpath = 'coreldraw essentials/' + prodver + '/ipm_cde';
			}
			//2021 Std
			else if (licid == '540111151' || licid == '540111144') {
				prodregpath = 'coreldraw standard/' + prodver + '/ipm_cdstd';
			}
			//2020 or 2021 SE
			else if (licid == '540111157' || licid == '540111154' || licid == '540231406') {
				prodregpath = 'coreldraw standard/' + prodver + '/ipm_cdse';
			}
			//2021 Designer
			else if (licid == '540111156' || licid == '540227267') {
				prodregpath = 'corel designer/' + prodver + '/ipm_cdts';
			}

			//check to see if we need to add Skip button (ONLY for offline hybrid DVD and offline long corp)
			location.href = "pcucmd://validate?param=\"/registry/regkey[@name='hklm/software/corel/" + prodregpath + "/premiumfeatures/CCC/serverdata']/regval[@name='x-channel'][contains(@value,'dvd')] OR /registry/regkey[@name='hklm/software/wow6432node/corel/" + prodregpath + "/premiumfeatures/CCC/serverdata']/regval[@name='x-channel'][contains(@value,'dvd')]\"";
			location.href = "pcucmd://CallScriptFunc?condition=true&funcname=showbtn&param=skipbtnhtml";
			location.href = "pcucmd://CallScriptFunc?condition=false&funcname=checksnlen";

			//check to see if we need to add Already Purchased button (ONLY for online/offline trials)
			location.href = "pcucmd://validate?param=/productmanifest/licenseinfolist/licenseinfo[(@licenseid='540111147' or @licenseid='540111151' or @licenseid='540111156') and @sourceid!='410030' and (@serialtype='8' or @serialtype='10')]";
			location.href = "pcucmd://CallScriptFunc?condition=true&funcname=showbtn&param=alreadypurbtnhtml";
		}
		document.getElementById(heading).style.display = 'block';
		location = 'pcucmd://FrameDataLoaded';
	}
	
	function privcheckboxes() {
		document.getElementById('CritSWUpdateCheckbox').checked = false;
		document.getElementById('CorelResearchCheckbox').checked = false;
	}

	function checksnlen() {
		location.href = "pcucmd://replacetoken?callback='rpt'&string='<PSN>'";
		if (g_tokens.length > 28) {
			showbtn('skipbtnhtml');
		}
		g_tokens = '';
	}

	//add the skip or already purchased buttons
	function showbtn(btntype) 
	{
		//get HTML of new button to be added
		var newbtnhtml = document.getElementById(btntype).innerHTML;
		if (newbtnhtml != null && newbtnhtml != '')
		{
			//button bar container
			var btnbarcont = parent.document.getElementById('ButtonBar').children[0];
			if (btnbarcont != null && btnbarcont != '')
			{
				var newbtnrow = '';
				//Skip button needs to be on the right (already purchased on the left)
				if (btntype == 'skipbtnhtml') {
					newbtnrow = btnbarcont.children[1].children[0].children[0].children[0];
				}
				else {
					newbtnrow = btnbarcont.children[0].children[0].children[0].children[0];
				}

				//add new button cell and html
				if (newbtnrow != null && newbtnrow != '') {
					var newbtncell = newbtnrow.insertCell(0);
					newbtncell.innerHTML = newbtnhtml;
				}
			}
		}
	}

	function showhide(el)
	{
		clearErrorMsg();
		var div_forgotpassword = document.getElementById('div_forgotpassword');
		var div_country = document.getElementById('div_country');
		var div_updates = document.getElementById('updates');
		var div_research = document.getElementById('research');
		if (el == 'haveacct' || el == 'subsc') {
			el = document.getElementById('haveacct');
			el.checked = true;
		}
		if (el.checked == true) {
			//hide acct creation fields
			div_forgotpassword.style.display = 'block';
			confirmpassword.parentElement.style.display = 'none';
			div_country.style.display = 'none';
			div_updates.style.display = 'none';
			div_research.style.display = 'none';
			//show "sign in" title and hide "let us get to know you" title
			document.getElementById('hd1').style.display = 'none';
			document.getElementById('hd2').style.display = 'block';
		}
		else {
			//show acct creation fields
			div_forgotpassword.style.display = 'none';
			confirmpassword.parentElement.style.display = 'block';
			div_country.style.display = 'block';
			div_updates.style.display = 'block';
			div_research.style.display = 'block';
			//hide "sign in" title and show "let us get to know you" title
			document.getElementById('hd1').style.display = 'block';
			document.getElementById('hd2').style.display = 'none';
		}
	}

	//is user signing in or creating account?
	function nextstep () {
		//logging in
		if (haveacct.checked == true) {
			logon('signin');
		}
		//creating acct
		else {
			validate('create');
		}
	}
	
	function CheckCred(type,input) {
		var str;
		//email
		if (type == 'e') {
			str = /^[A-Za-z0-9!#$%&'*+\/=?^_`{|}~-]+(?:\.[A-Za-z0-9!#$%&'*+\/=?^_`{|}~-]+)*@(?:[A-Za-z0-9](?:[A-Za-z0-9-]*[A-Za-z0-9])?\.)+[A-Za-z0-9](?:[A-Za-z0-9-]*[A-Za-z0-9])?$/;
		}
		//password
		else if (type == 'p') {
			str = /^([^ '"]{6,32})$/;
		}
		if (str != undefined)
		{
			if(str.test(input)) {
				return true;
			}
			else {
				return false;
			}
		}
	}

	function validate(type)
	{
		clearErrorMsg();
		//assume good
		g_bError = false;
		preValidate();
		var success = true;
		var errors = "";
		if (g_bError == false)
		{
			if( !CheckCred('e',username.value)) {
				success = false;
				errors += document.getElementById('errorstr_bademail').innerText + "\n";
			}
			if( !CheckCred('p',password.value)) {
				success = false;
				errors += document.getElementById('errorstr_badpass').innerText + "\n";
			}
			if (type == 'create')
			{
				if( !CheckCred('p',confirmpassword.value)) {
					success = false;
					errors += document.getElementById('errorstr_badpassconf').innerText + "\n";
				}
				if(password.value != confirmpassword.value) {					
					success = false;
					errors += document.getElementById('errorstr_passmismatch').innerText + "\n";
				}
			}
			if(success == true)
			{
				if (type == 'create') {
					CreateAccount();
				}
			}
			else {
				processerror(errors);
			}
		}
	}

	function CreateAccount()
	{
		var SubscriptionID = getCookie("SubscriptionID");
		var crit = document.getElementById("CritSWUpdateCheckbox");
		var custR = document.getElementById("CorelResearchCheckbox");
		var vFlag = 0;
		
		if(crit.checked) {
			vFlag = vFlag | 3;
		}
		if(custR.checked) {
			vFlag = vFlag | 16;
		}

		var Nickname = "";
		var Language = getParamVal("language");

		g_bError = false;		
		location = "pcucmd://createAccount?username='" + username.value + "'&password='" + password.value + "'&nickname='" + Nickname + "'&langcode='" + Language +  "'&countrycode='" + document.getElementById("countrySelector").value + "'&flags='" + vFlag + "'&onerror=processerror";

		if (!g_bError) {
			logon('create');
		}
	}
	
	function OnPrivacy() {
		location = "pcucmd://fullbrowse?url='<CorelComServer>/privacy'";
	}
	
	//clear error message field
	function clearErrorMsg() {
		error_msg.style.display = "none";
	}

	function preValidate() {
		//make sure username or password are not empty
		if (username.value == "" || password.value == "") {
			var errorstr_empty = document.getElementById('errorstr_empty').innerText;
			processerror(errorstr_empty);
		}
		//make sure username is a string and lower-case
		else {
			username.value = username.value.toString().toLowerCase();
		}
	}

	function IsUnderMaintenance()
	{
		//to from time are defined as EST time
		var dateFromEst = new Date(2022, 4 - 1, 23, 00, 00, 00 );  // -1 because months are from 0 to 11
		var dateFromUTC = new Date(dateFromEst.getTime() + 5 * 60 * 60 *1000) // TO UTC time
		var dateToEst = new Date(2022, 4 - 1, 24, 00, 00, 00 );
		var dateToUTC = new Date(dateToEst.getTime() + 5 * 60 * 60 *1000) // TO UTC time 

		var dateNow = new Date();
		var dateNowUTC = new Date(dateNow.getTime()+dateNow.getTimezoneOffset()*60*1000);

		if( (dateNowUTC > dateFromUTC) && (dateNowUTC < dateToUTC)) 
		{
			return true;
		}
		return false;
	}
	function IsUnknownError(strError)
	{
	   var ipmErrorMsg = "Error: Unknown Error.";
	   if(strError == ipmErrorMsg) {
			return true;
	   }
	   else
	   {
		   var language = getParamVal("lang");
		   language = language.toLowerCase();
		   switch (language)
		   {
			case "br":
				ipmErrorMsg = "Erro: Erro desconhecido.";
				break;
			case "cs":
				ipmErrorMsg = "错误: 未知错误。";
				break;
			case "ct":
				ipmErrorMsg = "错误: 未知错误。";
				break;
			case "cz":
				ipmErrorMsg = "Chyba: Neznámá chyba.";
				break;
			case "da":
				ipmErrorMsg = "Fejl: Ukendt fejl.";
				break;
			case "de":
				ipmErrorMsg ="Fehler: Unbekannter Fehler.";
				break;
			case "es":
				ipmErrorMsg ="Error: Error desconocido.";
				break;
			case "fr":
				ipmErrorMsg = "Erreur inconnue";
				break;
			case "it":
				ipmErrorMsg = "Errore: errore sconosciuto";
				break;			
			case "jp":
				ipmErrorMsg = "エラー: 不明なエラー";
				break;	
			case "kr":
				ipmErrorMsg = "오류: 알 수 없는 오류입니다.";
				break;
			case "ma":
				ipmErrorMsg = "Hiba: ismeretlen hiba.";
				break;		
			case "nl":
				ipmErrorMsg ="Fout: onbekende fout.";
				break;
			case "no":
				ipmErrorMsg = "Feil: Ukjent feil.";
				break;	
			case "pl":
				ipmErrorMsg ="Błąd: nieznany błąd.";
				break;
			case "po":
				ipmErrorMsg ="Erro: Erro desconhecido.";
				break;
			case "ru":
				ipmErrorMsg ="Ошибка. Неизвестная ошибка.";
				break;
			case "su":	
				ipmErrorMsg = "Virhe: Tuntematon virhe.";
				break;		
			case "sv":
				ipmErrorMsg = "Fel: okänt fel.";
				break;
			case "tr":	
				ipmErrorMsg = "Hata: Tanımlanamayan Hata.";
				break;
			}
			if(strError == ipmErrorMsg) {
				return true;
			}
		}
		return false;
	}

	//error handling
	function processerror(strError) {
		g_bError = true;
		var strMaintenanceErrorDesc = "Corel’s authentication service is currently under planned maintenance. Please try again later.";
		var language = getParamVal("lang");
		language = language.toLowerCase();
		switch(language)
		{
			case "br":
				strMaintenanceErrorDesc = "No momento, o serviço de autenticação da Corel está em manutenção planejada. Tente novamente mais tarde.";
				break;
			case "cs":
				strMaintenanceErrorDesc = "Corel 的验证服务目前正在计划维护中。请稍后再试。";
				break;
			case "ct":
				strMaintenanceErrorDesc = "Corel 驗證服務目前正進行預定維護，請稍後再試一次。";
				break;
			case "cz":
				strMaintenanceErrorDesc = "Probíhá plánovaná údržba ověřovací služby Corel. Zkuste to později.";
				break;
			case "de":
				strMaintenanceErrorDesc = "Der Authentifizierungsdienst von Corel wird derzeit planmäßig gewartet. Bitte versuchen Sie es später noch einmal.";
				break;
			case "es":
				strMaintenanceErrorDesc = "Se está llevando a cabo el mantenimiento del servicio de autenticación de Corel. Inténtalo de nuevo más adelante.";
				break;
			case "fr":
				strMaintenanceErrorDesc = "Le service d'authentification Corel est actuellement en cours de maintenance planifiée. Veuillez réessayer ultérieurement.";
				break;
			case "it":
				strMaintenanceErrorDesc = "Il servizio di autenticazione Corel è attualmente sotto manutenzione pianificata. Riprova più tardi.";
				break;			
			case "jp":
				strMaintenanceErrorDesc = "Corel の認証サービスは、ただ今定期的メンテナンスの実行中です。後ほどもう一度お試しください。";
				break;		
			case "nl":
				strMaintenanceErrorDesc = "De verificatieservice van Corel ondergaat momenteel gepland onderhoud. Probeer het later opnieuw.";
				break;
			case "pl":
				strMaintenanceErrorDesc = "Aktualnie trwa planowa konserwacja usługi uwierzytelnienia firmy Corel. Spróbuj ponownie później.";
				break;
			case "ru":
				strMaintenanceErrorDesc = "В настоящий момент служба аутентификации Corel находится в режиме запланированного техобслуживания. Пожалуйста, повторите попытку позднее.";
				break;	
			case "sv":
				strMaintenanceErrorDesc = "Corels autentiseringstjänst undergår planerat underhåll. Försök igen senare.";
				break;
			case "tr":	
				strMaintenanceErrorDesc = "Corel'in kimlik doğrulama hizmeti şu anda planlı bakım sürecindedir. Lütfen daha sonra tekrar deneyin.";
				break;
		}
		var strErrorDesc = strError;
		if( IsUnknownError(strError) )
		{
			if(IsUnderMaintenance()) {
				strErrorDesc = strMaintenanceErrorDesc;
			}
		}
		else
		{
			var nIndex = strError.indexOf("|");
			var strErrorcode;
			if (nIndex >= 0) {
				strErrorDesc = strErrorDesc.substr(nIndex + 1);
				strErrorCode = strError.substr(0, nIndex);
				if( strErrorCode == "999" || strErrorCode == "1000"  )
				{
					if(IsUnderMaintenance())
					{
						strErrorDesc = strMaintenanceErrorDesc;
					}
				}
			}
		}
		error_msg.style.display = "block";
		error_msg.innerText = strErrorDesc;
	}

	//logging in
	function logon(type) {
		clearErrorMsg();
		//assume good
		g_bError = false;
		if (type == 'signin') {
			validate(type);
		}
		if (g_bError == false)
		{
			location.href = "pcucmd://authenticate?username='" + username.value + "'&password='" + password.value + "'&showpsid='true'&onerror='processerror'";
			if (g_bError == false) {
				loginsuccess();
			}
		}
	}

	//successfully logged in
	function loginsuccess() {
		location = "pcucmd://Next";
	}
</script>

	//global vars
